     <p>
      The following is a
      <b>
       list of zombie
       <a href="/wiki/Feature_film" title="Feature film">
        feature films
       </a>
      </b>
      .
      <a href="/wiki/Zombie" title="Zombie">
       Zombies
      </a>
      are fictional creatures usually portrayed as reanimated corpses or virally infected human beings. They are commonly enacted as
      <a href="/wiki/Cannibalism" title="Cannibalism">
       cannibalistic
      </a>
      in nature. While zombie films generally fall into the
      <a href="/wiki/Horror_film" title="Horror film">
       horror
      </a>
      genre, some cross over into other genres, such as
      <a href="/wiki/Comedy_film" title="Comedy film">
       comedy
      </a>
      ,
      <a href="/wiki/Science_fiction_film" title="Science fiction film">
       science fiction
      </a>
      ,
      <a href="/wiki/Thriller_(genre)" title="Thriller (genre)">
       thriller
      </a>
      , or
      <a href="/wiki/Romance_film" title="Romance film">
       romance
      </a>
      . Distinct subgenres have evolved, such as the "
      <a href="/wiki/Zombie_comedy" title="Zombie comedy">
       zombie comedy
      </a>
      " or the "
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Zombie_apocalypse" title="Zombie apocalypse">
       zombie apocalypse
      </a>
      ". Zombies are distinct from
      <a href="/wiki/Ghost" title="Ghost">
       ghosts
      </a>
      ,
      <a href="/wiki/Ghoul" title="Ghoul">
       ghouls
      </a>
      ,
      <a href="/wiki/Mummy" title="Mummy">
       mummies
      </a>
      , or
      <a href="/wiki/Vampire" title="Vampire">
       vampires
      </a>
      , so this list does not include films devoted to these types of undead.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEKay200850.E2.80.9353.2C_323.E2.80.93332_1-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEKay200850.E2.80.9353.2C_323.E2.80.93332-1">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        1
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      <a href="/wiki/Victor_Hugo_Halperin" title="Victor Hugo Halperin">
       Victor Halperin
      </a>
      's
      <i>
       <a href="/wiki/White_Zombie_(film)" title="White Zombie (film)">
        White Zombie
       </a>
      </i>
      was released in 1932 and is often cited to be the first zombie film.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-white_zombie_A_2-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-white_zombie_A-2">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        2
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-white_zombie_C_3-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-white_zombie_C-3">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        3
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
